---
title: "Where's the draft of the post I just wrote?"
date: 2013-10-05
forum: Forum Feedback &amp; Help
---

### Post by Archelon on 2013-10-05
It effectively vanished into the ether when I clicked [FONT=system]Preview[/FONT].  Apparently I was logged out while I was writing it; the [FONT=system]back[/FONT] button got it back, and then logging in (in a different browser tab, of course) somehow caused the repeat of the same action to disappear it permanently.  But the whole time I was writing it a yellow message would inform me every few seconds that it had been saved.  So how do I get it back?

---

### Post by Elfy on 2013-10-05
at the bottom of the post should be a 'restore autosave' message

---

### Post by SeijiSensei on 2013-10-05
If you use Firefox, I recommend installing the [Lazarus](http://getlazarus.com/) add-on.  It will save texts from all forms.  If you lose a posting, right-click in the composition window and choose Recover Text.  Works in all forms, not just ones with autosave features like vBulletin 4.

---

There are language filters and moderators that edit.

### Post by cariboo on 2013-10-05
It looks like the op is trying to drag and drop images in Firefox, which is a known FIrefox bug. I'd suggest he either use an image hosting service, or use the attachment facility available in the advanced editor.

The forum does have a censored word list, as we have users of all ages, this is a family friendly forum
